\doxysubsection{函数说明}
\Hypertarget{namespacehello__world_1_1devices_1_1referee_a30f1e50d6e85c306486883a0668b7f50}\label{namespacehello__world_1_1devices_1_1referee_a30f1e50d6e85c306486883a0668b7f50} 
\index{hello\_world::devices::referee@{hello\_world::devices::referee}!GetCrc16CheckSum@{GetCrc16CheckSum}}
\index{GetCrc16CheckSum@{GetCrc16CheckSum}!hello\_world::devices::referee@{hello\_world::devices::referee}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GetCrc16CheckSum()}{GetCrc16CheckSum()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily uint16\+\_\+t hello\+\_\+world\+::devices\+::referee\+::\+Get\+Crc16\+Check\+Sum (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+message,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{length,  }\item[{uint16\+\_\+t}]{crc16\+\_\+init }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Calculate and return the CRC16 checksum of a message. 

This function iterates through the input message and computes the CRC16 checksum using the provided CRC16 initialization value.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em p\+\_\+message} & Pointer to the message data. \\
\hline
{\em length} & Length of the message in bytes. \\
\hline
{\em crc8\+\_\+init} & Initial CRC16 value to start the checksum calculation. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
Calculated CRC16 checksum for the message. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily uint8\+\_\+t hello\+\_\+world\+::devices\+::referee\+::\+Get\+Crc8\+Check\+Sum (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+message,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{length,  }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{crc8\+\_\+init }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Calculate and return the CRC8 checksum of a message. 

This function iterates through the input message and computes the CRC8 checksum using the provided CRC8 initialization value.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em p\+\_\+message} & Pointer to the message data. \\
\hline
{\em length} & Length of the message in bytes. \\
\hline
{\em crc8\+\_\+init} & Initial CRC8 value to start the checksum calculation. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
uint8\+\_\+t 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em Calculated} & CRC8 checksum for the message. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
